My wife and I are not from Fresno, but our son goes to Fresno State and we like to stay near him for a month or two throughout the year(he doesn't feel the same way).  We take our RV here to avoid the costs of hotels.  Its a quiet place and the showers and pool seems to be cleaned fairly often.  After checking out the other parks, this one seemed to be the best value so far in the Fresno area.<//Review>

Buster Weedmire</user_name>
<date>1385174374265</date><Rating>3<//Rating>< text>
RV usage:
For the pricing it's decent for a monthly rate. Have found it to be safe here.
Wifi is decent from my experience.
Maintenance folks respond quickly to issues.
Half RV park and half mobile home park.
Not a new park, but it's not trashy.
A mix of RVers mostly for work related longer stays.
Area can be noisy at night; frequent trains (q1h almost) and proximity to freeway.
Neighbors are generally quiet at night.<//text>

This is a heated cycling studio... I always snag a bike near the door, so whenever the door opens, I get a wisp of cool air.     We started late due to an unfortunate circumstance next door got ran into by a car just 30min prior, and I was new and needed adjustment.   Irina gave us still the full workout time plus some.   Another plus, they provide free towels and shoe rental!!!!    Free towels, free shoe rental, free water just bring your own bottle because you will need that refill!   Amazing!!!   Believe me, you will need that towel, you will need those shoes, and you will need that water!  Parking is easy, ample and free!  I don't feel claustrophobic in the parking lot or in class.  I love Irina's ENTHUSIASM when she teaches, it pumps you up!  Daniel... you kill me every time.   He does all these things that require your core.    I HAVE NO CORE... I have no balance, so even though the bike is stationary, I'm scared for myself.   But, I have gotten better, maybe even a little stronger I might add.  So yeah, I totally recommend this place!   I love this humble mom and pop studio, no pretentiousness here, just come as you are and get your workout on.< /Review>

<Rate>4< /Rate>< review>
Class Pass taught me‚Ä¶.

The Price: First class is $10 for new customers then $17 per class after.

Location: Super cute and cozy area in a strip mall. The setup is a bit odd in that you walk in to the check in desk and must travel through the cycling arena to get to the lockers and bathroom. The locker area is spacious and bright which contrasts with the dark cycling arena. But all in all there‚Äôs plenty of room and never felt things were overcrowded. Plus there‚Äôs plenty of parking which is a major plus.

The Workout: My bike‚Äôs console was broken so I wasn‚Äôt able to keep up with the different gears but I tried my best to adjust and still had a great workout. The instructor had great energy and kept everyone motivated. The room was a bit warm but great for those who love to sweat. The back of the room gets hotter so if you are afraid of overheating then make your way closer to the front.  But above all else, the music was SUPER good! The workout featured a great mix of hip hop and some pop, but mostly Beyonc√©.

But overall Finergy Cycle provides a great workout at a reasonable price. The class wasn‚Äôt overcrowded and customer service was on point. Also they don‚Äôt charge for a spin shoe rental which is a major plus. Online they do mention a towel rental fee but they didn‚Äôt charge my boyfriend so it may be fine not to bring one. But you will sweat so keep that in mind and make sure to bring plenty of water.< /review>

Overall I do not recommend the "garlic bread" pizza; it is way too thin for what I would want in garlic bread, and they don't cut their garlic cloves. A pizza is as it‚Äôs, just a pizza for everyone. It‚Äôs affordable, it‚Äôs quick, it‚Äôs tasty, it really is delicious. The pie style is thin, with a proper load of ingredients on top. One pie is easily enough to fill up one person and splitting two is a good way to experience a little diversity.

We ordered the Margarita and the BBQ chicken pizza. The 9inch pie is a great bang for your buck, it was delicious. The chicken was extremely well marinated, the cheese was perfectly melted, what more could you really ask for at a price point like this? The crust is organic; definitely a unique find for San Francisco.

A Margarita pizza will run you 3$ and a BBQ, will set you back 7$. This place is a must go for pizza lovers in SF. At a price point like this, how could you resist?< /text>

< text>
In San Francisco, I pay over a thousand dollars a month to sleep in somebody's living room. I guess I can't complain though, because apizza has $2.75 personal margherita pizzas! In a city where everything costs an arm and a leg (and some other body parts), this place has the NERVE to sell affordable pizzas made with organic dough and organic sauce and some of the fastest, friendliest service I've ever experienced. They also have three kinds of oil "spritz", and for some reason, a recording of a cackling baby in the bathroom. Is the pizza here the best I've ever had? Not even close. Is this place weird, cheap, and tasty enough for me to write a paragraph long caption about and strongly recommend? Absolutely.</text>

< review>
It's all about the value here.  For $2.75--yes $2.75!--I had a fine Margherita pizza that was very tasty and fresh out of the oven.  Granted it's not quite up to Delifina around the corner, but for 1/5 the price it is seriously worth eating!  The staff is super nice and almost all French folks with their charming accents.  They offer the requisite shakers of oregano, hot pepper and Parmesan, plus real knives and forks for civilized eating.  Ironically, my Diet Coke costs almost exactly as much as my pizza!  (They gotta make some profit somewhere.) But this concept is a winner.</review>

The latest one had to transfer me to someone who --from her lack of words-- was not informed as to what I wanted to know.
When asked what the cake had, like icing and all, I had to be placed on hold for them to be able to later tell me it was made of a vanilla cake, mango filling, and mango on top.

Now, upon arrival today, and in asking for the mango cake, the young lady at the counter had mistakenly heard that I wanted some kind of mango shake.
I know, I know...you are thinking, "They sound the same." But their product is not called a "shake"!
Once it was made clear with my slow, precise and careful enunciation of "cake," I was immediately charged and offered to join some rewards group via their counter top tablet. I declined to join.
Then the young lady asked, "Would you like anything written on it?"
"Sure. Yes," I thought with excitement for my Mother to see something written on her long desired birthday mango cake from Goldilocks.

Cashier, having taken my signed receipt, and given me my copy, goes to the cake with out any hesitation or thought to stop at the sink she was passing to wash her hands.
*slaps forehead*

< review>
Sister Bear & Brother Bear had a disagreement

Brother Bear decided to rebrand existing Goldilocks restaurants as Leelin Bakery & Cafes.

Sister Bear later branched out & opened up new Goldilocks restaurants in Cerritos, West Covina & National City.

Rodney Bear is happy to have Goldilocks back & still in my hood!

Goldilocks is like the Filipino Porto's.  Various baked goods are available for purchase.
Hopia
Siopao (warm & refrigerated)
Ensaymada
Cakes
My favorite, bread!

On a cold Saturday, we were famished & needed a hot meal.  A sign said "Wait to be seated", but I spied many open tables to eat, so after waiting for a minute or two, I decided we should seat ourselves.  A quick glance at the menu led to our lunch choices-

Mami siomai
Hot soup with egg noodles, celery, green onions, carrots, hardboiled egg & 3 pork siomai.  Soup for the soul.  I was a little disappointed that only 3 siomai were in the soup, but they were delicious.  The egg noodles were long & chewy, the broth soothing & comforting.  An OK dish

Lechon kawali
Crispy pork goodness!  I enjoyed how there weren't too many hard bits of fatty pork, like most turo turo restaurants have.  The meat was tender & the fat sweet,  Dipped in lechon sauce, and it's a beautiful thing!  But, who's kidding who?  It's all about that crunchy skin, baby!  Just be careful biting down on it.  Those w/o strong chompers may chip a tooth, know what I'm sayin?

Dishes are a la carte & do not come with rice.  Also, there are currently no lunch specials to be had.  All the Goldilocks favorites are here, such as bagoong fried rice, calamari & their sizzling sisig.

Service was okay.  It seems the staff is still oiling out all the kinks.  The wait wasn't horrible, but not quick, either.  Plenty of table seating on the left side of the restaurant, the right being dedicated to the bakery goods.  Parking is at the Seafood City shopping plaza, which can get quite busy during the weekend.

Like bumping into an old friend, Goldilocks is back & just the same as I remembered.  I'm fortunate to have had a Goldilocks nearby all my life, from the location that was previously located on Pioneer Blvd, to it's strategic move to South & Gridley.  This Goldilocks has prime real estate in a plaza catering to the Filipino community, with Seafood City, Valerio's, Jollibee & Eriel's Caf√© as neighbors.  Come by for a authentic Filipino meal, then pick up some bread or other baked goods to take home.

Rodney Bear highly recommends!
NOMNOMNOMNOMNOMNOMNOMNOMNOMNOM</review>

<Rating>4<//Rating>< Text>
Great sports bar with even better chicken wings!

We stopped here on a Thursday night to eat wings and watch football. The menu of wing flavors is extensive and covers everything from mild to extreme heat. I opted for the Green Machine flavor (medium heat and combination of cilantro, guacamole, Serrano, and jalape√±o) and also the El Diablo (hot heat, blend of 3 spices). They were both fantastic!

I also ordered the chicken blue cheese tater tots which were very good. Perhaps a side of hot sauce with these would have helped.

The beer selection was great, and our server was super friendly and attentive. There are TV's everywhere so you always had a view regardless of where you sit. We were sat at a long table shared with some others, but still had plenty of space to relax.

I'd definitely come back!< /Text>

<review>Good wing places come in 2 varieties: they cook the wings excellently or they have amazing sauce.

Dirty birds is the latter. The wings themselves were quality - as in freshness and size - but personally I prefer a fried to order wing. These were clearly baked beforehand amd then flash fried to order. Huge benefit to this is time though. My order of wings was out I  about 10 minutes despite it being a packed Friday night.

The sauces, though! A large selection of great sauces. About 40. I tried 3 and all were excellent. Particularly the honey mustard and habanero. Great roasted hab flavor without the heat being over-powering which is a very difficult line to walk on.

I would come back any time I'm in SD.<//review><Rating>5<//Rating><Gmap_id>0x80deab031fe40001:0xea41598717ead4ea< /Gmap_id><pictures>None< /pictures><Resp>None</Resp></record>
